You will almost find a lot at least 70 players connected to the server. As time passes, it will replace FIBS by creating multiple clients on different devices (desktop, phones, smart TVs).\r\n\r\nThe user interface is now highly optimized for speed and for saving your battery.\r\n\r\nManual rolls. Unique feature for those of you that think the dices are not random:\r\nThe formula explains by itself:\r\n   dice = 1 + (millis mod 6)\r\nMillis change 1000 times per second.
